  7. ‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° ‚Äú‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‚Äù

10.4 ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì Next PM Date

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏≥ PM ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à: - Is Fixed Date = true: Next PM = Last PM Date + Frequency Days - Is Fixed Date = false: Next PM = Today + Frequency Days

11. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Troubleshooting

11.1 Database Connection Error

‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤:

‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç: 1. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö SQL Server Service ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà 2. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö Connection String ‡πÉ‡∏ô .env 3. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö Firewall Port 1433

11.2 Port Already in Use

‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤:

‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç:

‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç: 1. ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ https://localhost:5006 ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á 2. Accept Certificate Warning 3. ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏≤ Frontend

A. ‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå

‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢

1. ‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏≥

1.1 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏ñ‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πå

‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏â‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á API (Application Programming Interface) ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏≥‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô (Preventive Maintenance Management System) ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô API ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á

1.2 ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏ï

‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏∏‡∏° API ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö Backend ‡∏ã‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢: - ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô (User Management) - ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏à‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏£ (Machine Management) - ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏≥‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏≤ (PM Plan Management) - ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏≥‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏≤ (PM Recording) - ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥ (Reports & Dashboard)

1.3 ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£

  • ‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏±‡∏í‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö (Developers)

3. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô (Authentication)

‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ JWT (JSON Web Token) ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡πà‡∏á Token ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÉ‡∏ô HTTP Header ‡∏î‡∏±‡∏á‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ:

4. API Endpoints

4.1 Authentication API

4.1.1 ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏π‡πà‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö (Login)

‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î

‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô ‚ùå ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á

  "username": "admin",
  "password": "password123"
}

Response ‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à (200 OK):

{
  "token": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9...",
  "user": {
    "id": 1,
    "username": "admin",
    "name": "‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö",
    "systemRole": "ADMIN",
    "permissionType": "ALL",
    "role": "Admin"
  }
}

Response ‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î (401 Unauthorized):

  "error": "Invalid credentials"
}

4.1.2 ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô

‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î

‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô ‚úÖ ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á

  "id": 1,
  "username": "admin",
  "name": "‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö",

4.2 User Master API

4.2.1 ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î

‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î

1. ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° Environment Variables

1.1 ‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤

‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå ‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢

1.2 ‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ Variables ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î

Variable ‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢

2. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ Database

2.1 ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Connection String

DATABASE_URL="sqlserver://HOST:PORT;database=DATABASE_NAME;user=USERNAME;password=PASSWORD;encrypt=true;trustServerCertificate=true"

2.2 ‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå

‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á
HOST IP ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Hostname ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á SQL Server localhost, 192.168.1.100
PORT Port ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á SQL Server 1433 (Default)
DATABASE_NAME ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ Database maintenance_pm_db
USERNAME ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Database sa, pm_user
PASSWORD ‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Database YourSecurePassword

2.3 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏°

Option ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤
encrypt ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ true / false
trustServerCertificate ‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Self-signed Certificate true / false
connectionTimeout Timeout ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ (ms) 30000

2.4 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á Connection String

Local Development:

DATABASE_URL="sqlserver://localhost:1433;database=maintenance_pm_db;user=sa;password=MyPassword123;encrypt=true;trustServerCertificate=true"

Production (Remote Server):

DATABASE_URL="sqlserver://192.168.1.100:1433;database=pm_production;user=pm_user;password=SecureP@ssw0rd;encrypt=true;trustServerCertificate=false"

Named Instance:

DATABASE_URL="sqlserver://SERVER_NAME\\INSTANCE_NAME:1433;database=pm_db;user=sa;password=Password123;encrypt=true;trustServerCertificate=true"

‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠ ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢

‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ã‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô ‡∏ú‡∏™‡∏° ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Ç ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏ì‡πå
‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏ú‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Commit ‡∏•‡∏á Git
‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô Token ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î

3.3 ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Secret Key

‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 1: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Node.js

4. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ Server

‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏™‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô

5. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ Email (SMTP)

5.2 ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î

Variable ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á

SMTP_PORT SMTP Port 587 (TLS), 465 (SSL), 25 (No Encryption)
SMTP_USER Username/Email ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Login noreply@company.com
SMTP_PASS Password ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ App Password your-app-password
EMAIL_FROM ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á "PM System <noreply@company.com>"

5.3 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á SMTP Settings

Gmail:

SMTP_HOST=smtp.gmail.com
SMTP_PORT=587
SMTP_USER=your-email@gmail.com
SMTP_PASS=your-app-password
EMAIL_FROM="PM Notification <your-email@gmail.com>"

‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏: ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Gmail ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ App Password ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô Password ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á

Office 365:

SMTP_PORT=587
SMTP_USER=noreply@company.onmicrosoft.com
SMTP_PASS=your-password
EMAIL_FROM="PM System <noreply@company.onmicrosoft.com>"

Internal SMTP (No Auth):

SMTP_HOST=mail.internal.company.com
SMTP_PORT=25
SMTP_USER=
SMTP_PASS=
EMAIL_FROM="PM System <pm@company.com>"

6. ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ Frontend

8.2 ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö Database Connection

npx prisma db pull

‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à = Connection ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á

8.3 ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö SMTP

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Script ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö:

const nodemailer = require('nodemailer');

const transporter = nodemailer.createTransport({
  host: process.env.SMTP_HOST,
  port: process.env.SMTP_PORT,
  auth: {
    user: process.env.SMTP_USER,
    pass: process.env.SMTP_PASS
  }
});

transporter.sendMail({
  from: process.env.EMAIL_FROM,
  to: 'test@example.com',
  subject: 'Test Email',
  text: 'This is a test email.'
}).then(() => console.log('Email sent successfully'))
  .catch(err => console.error('Email error:', err));

üìé Security Best Practices

‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥

‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠ ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥
1 ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° Commit ‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå .env ‡∏•‡∏á Git
2 ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Environment Variables ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô Hardcode
3 ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô JWT_SECRET ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ã‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô
4 ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Strong Password ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Database
5 ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå Database User ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î
6 Encrypt ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ Database (encrypt=true)
7 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ Firewall ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°
